   * ye nāsvāditapūrviṇo mṛdudhiyaḥ śrīpratyabhijñāmṛtaṃ tenātrādhikṛtāḥ	* ye na-AsvAdita-pUrviNaH mRduDiyaH SrI-pratyaBijQA-amRtam tena-atra-aDikRtAH
   paraiḥ punar idaṃ pūrṇāśayaiś carvyatām || VSpkC_4.2:6	parEH punar idam pUrNa-ASayEH carvyatAm || VSpkC_4.2:6
   * śivādikṣityanto vitatavitato yo 'dhvavibhavaḥ	* Siva-Adi-kziti-antaH vitata-vitataH yaH aDva-viBavaH
   sphurannānāsargasthitilayadaśācitritatanuḥ /	sPurat-nAnA-sarga-sTiti-laya-daSA-citrita-tanuH /
   * iyadviśvaṃ yasya prasarakaṇikāsau vijayate paraḥ saṃvitspando	* iyat-viSvam yasya prasara-kaNikA-asO vijayate paraH saMvid-spandaH-
   lasadasamasaukhyāyatanabhūḥ || VSpkC_4.2:7]	lasat-asama-sOKya-Ayatana-BUH || VSpkC_4.2:7]
